186→}\n   187→\n   188→// markUpdatedPodsReady manually marks updated Deployment pods status to ready,\n   189→// until the deployment is complete\n   190→func (d *deploymentTester) markUpdatedPodsReady(wg *sync.WaitGroup) {\n   191→\tdefer wg.Done()\n   192→\n   193→\tns := d.deployment.Namespace\n   194→\terr := wait.PollImmediate(pollInterval, pollTimeout, func() (bool, error) {\n   195→\t\t// We're done when the deployment is complete\n   196→\t\tif completed, err := d.deploymentComplete(); err != nil {\n   197→\t\t\treturn false, err\n   198→\t\t} else if completed {\n   199→\t\t\treturn true, nil\n   200→\t\t}\n   201→\t\t// Otherwise, mark remaining pods as ready\n   202→\t\tpods, err := d.listUpdatedPods()\n   203→\t\tif err != nil {\n   204→\t\t\td.t.Log(err)\n   205→\t\t\treturn false, nil\n   206→\t\t}\n   207→\t\td.t.Logf(\"%d/%d of deployment pods are created\", len(pods), *d.deployment.Spec.Replicas)\n   208→\t\tfor i := range pods {\n   209→\t\t\tpod := pods[i]\n   210→\t\t\tif podutil.IsPodReady(&pod) {\n   211→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   212→\t\t\t}\n   213→\t\t\tif err = markPodReady(d.c, ns, &pod); err != nil {\n   214→\t\t\t\td.t.Logf(\"failed to update Deployment pod %s, will retry later: %v\", pod.Name, err)\n   215→\t\t\t}\n   216→\t\t}\n   217→\t\treturn false, nil\n   218→\t})\n   219→\tif err != nil {\n   220→\t\td.t.Errorf(\"failed to mark updated Deployment pods to ready: %v\", err)\n   221→\t}\n   222→}\n   223→\n   224→// removeTerminatedPods manually removes terminated Deployment pods,\n   225→// until the deployment is complete\n   226→func (d *deploymentTester) removeTerminatedPods(ctx context.Context, wg *sync.WaitGroup) {\n   227→\tdefer wg.Done()\n   228→\n   229→\terr := wait.PollUntilContextTimeout(ctx, pollInterval, pollTimeout, true, func(ctx context.Context) (bool, error) {\n   230→\t\t// We're done when the deployment is complete\n   231→\t\tif completed, err := d.deploymentComplete(); err != nil {\n   232→\t\t\treturn false, err\n   233→\t\t} else if completed {\n   234→\t\t\treturn true, nil\n   235→\t\t}\n   236→\t\t// Otherwise, mark remaining pods as ready\n   237→\t\trsList, err := deploymentutil.ListReplicaSets(d.deployment, deploymentutil.RsListFromClient(d.c.AppsV1()))\n   238→\t\tif err != nil {\n   239→\t\t\td.t.Log(err)\n   240→\t\t\treturn false, nil\n   241→\t\t}\n   242→\t\tfor _, rs := range rsList {\n   243→\t\t\tif err := d.removeRSPods(ctx, rs, math.MaxInt, true, 0); err != nil {\n   244→\t\t\t\td.t.Log(err)\n   245→\t\t\t\treturn false, nil\n   246→\t\t\t}\n   247→\t\t}\n   248→\t\treturn false, nil\n   249→\t})\n   250→\tif err != nil {\n   251→\t\td.t.Errorf(\"failed to remove terminated Deployment pods: %v\", err)\n   252→\t}\n   253→}\n   254→\n   255→func (d *deploymentTester) deploymentComplete() (bool, error) {\n   256→\tlatest, err := d.c.AppsV1().Deployments(d.deployment.Namespace).Get(context.TODO(), d.deployment.Name, metav1.GetOptions{})\n   257→\tif err != nil {\n   258→\t\treturn false, err\n   259→\t}\n   260→\treturn deploymentutil.DeploymentComplete(d.deployment, &latest.Status), nil\n   261→}\n   262→\n   263→// Waits for the deployment to complete, and check rolling update strategy isn't broken at any times.\n   264→// Rolling update strategy should not be broken during a rolling update.\n   265→func (d *deploymentTester) waitForDeploymentCompleteAndCheckRolling() error {\n   266→\treturn testutil.WaitForDeploymentCompleteAndCheckRolling(d.c, d.deployment, d.t.Logf, pollInterval, pollTimeout)\n   267→}\n   268→\n   269→// Waits for the deployment to complete, and don't check if rolling update strategy is broken.\n   270→// Rolling update strategy is used only during a rolling update, and can be violated in other situations,\n   271→// such as shortly after a scaling event or the deployment is just created.\n   272→func (d *deploymentTester) waitForDeploymentComplete() error {\n   273→\treturn testutil.WaitForDeploymentComplete(d.c, d.deployment, d.t.Logf, pollInterval, pollTimeout)\n   274→}\n   275→\n   276→// waitForDeploymentCompleteAndCheckRollingAndMarkPodsReady waits for the Deployment to complete\n   277→// while marking updated Deployment pods as ready at the same time.\n   278→// Uses hard check to make sure rolling update strategy is not violated at any times.\n   279→func (d *deploymentTester) waitForDeploymentCompleteAndCheckRollingAndMarkPodsReady() error {\n   280→\tvar wg sync.WaitGroup\n   281→\n   282→\t// Manually mark updated Deployment pods as ready in a separate goroutine\n   283→\twg.Add(1)\n   284→\tgo d.markUpdatedPodsReady(&wg)\n   285→\t// Wait for goroutine to finish, for all return paths.\n   286→\tdefer wg.Wait()\n   287→\n   288→\t// Wait for the Deployment status to complete while Deployment pods are becoming ready\n   289→\terr := d.waitForDeploymentCompleteAndCheckRolling()\n   290→\tif err != nil {\n   291→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to wait for Deployment %s to complete: %v\", d.deployment.Name, err)\n   292→\t}\n   293→\n   294→\treturn nil\n   295→}\n   296→\n   297→// waitForDeploymentCompleteAndMarkPodsReady waits for the Deployment to complete\n   298→// while marking updated Deployment pods as ready at the same time.\n   299→func (d *deploymentTester) waitForDeploymentCompleteAndMarkPodsReady() error {\n   300→\tvar wg sync.WaitGroup\n   301→\n   302→\t// Manually mark updated Deployment pods as ready in a separate goroutine\n   303→\twg.Add(1)\n   304→\tgo d.markUpdatedPodsReady(&wg)\n   305→\n   306→\t// Wait for the Deployment status to complete using soft check, while Deployment pods are becoming ready\n   307→\terr := d.waitForDeploymentComplete()\n   308→\tif err != nil {\n   309→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to wait for Deployment status %s: %v\", d.deployment.Name, err)\n   310→\t}\n   311→\n   312→\t// Wait for goroutine to finish\n   313→\twg.Wait()\n   314→\n   315→\treturn nil\n   316→}\n   317→\n   318→// waitForDeploymentCompleteAndMarkPodsReadyAndRemoveTerminating waits for the Deployment to complete\n   319→// while marking updated Deployment pods as ready and removes terminated pods at the same time.\n   320→func (d *deploymentTester) waitForDeploymentCompleteAndMarkPodsReadyAndRemoveTerminated(ctx context.Context) error {\n   321→\tvar wg sync.WaitGroup\n   322→\n   323→\t// Manually mark updated Deployment pods as ready in a separate goroutine\n   324→\twg.Add(1)\n   325→\tgo d.markUpdatedPodsReady(&wg)\n   326→\n   327→\twg.Add(1)\n   328→\tgo d.removeTerminatedPods(ctx, &wg)\n   329→\n   330→\t// Wait for the Deployment status to complete using soft check, while Deployment pods are becoming ready\n   331→\terr := d.waitForDeploymentComplete()\n   332→\tif err != nil {\n   333→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to wait for Deployment status %s: %w\", d.deployment.Name, err)\n   334→\t}\n   335→\n   336→\t// Wait for goroutine to finish\n   337→\twg.Wait()\n   338→\n   339→\treturn nil\n   340→}\n   341→\n   342→func 490→\n   491→// waitForReadyReplicas waits for number of ready replicas to equal number of replicas.\n   492→func (d *deploymentTester) waitForDeploymentStatusReplicasFields(ctx context.Context, replicas, updatedReplicas, readyReplicas, availableReplicas, unavailableReplicas int32, terminatingReplicas *int32) error {\n   493→\tvar lastErr error\n   494→\terr := wait.PollUntilContextTimeout(ctx, pollInterval, pollTimeout, true, func(_ context.Context) (bool, error) {\n   495→\t\t// do not pass ctx to checkDeploymentStatusReplicasFields (Deployments().Get) so we always obtain the latest error and not the one from deadline exceeded\n   496→\t\tlastErr = d.checkDeploymentStatusReplicasFields(replicas, updatedReplicas, readyReplicas, availableReplicas, unavailableReplicas, terminatingReplicas)\n   497→\t\treturn lastErr == nil, nil\n   498→\t})\n   499→\tif err != nil {\n   500→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%w: %w\", lastErr, err)\n   501→\t}\n   502→\treturn nil\n   503→}\n   504→\n   505→// Verify all replicas fields of DeploymentStatus have desired count.\n   506→// Immediately return an error when found a non-matching replicas field.\n   507→func (d *deploymentTester) checkDeploymentStatusReplicasFields(replicas, updatedReplicas, readyReplicas, availableReplicas, unavailableReplicas int32, terminatingReplicas *int32) error {\n   508→\tdeployment, err := d.c.AppsV1().Deployments(d.deployment.Namespace).Get(context.TODO(), d.deployment.Name, metav1.GetOptions{})\n   509→\tif err != nil {\n   510→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to get deployment %q: %v\", d.deployment.Name, err)\n   511→\t}\n   512→\tif deployment.Status.Replicas != replicas {\n   513→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected .replicas: expect %d, got %d\", replicas, deployment.Status.Replicas)\n   514→\t}\n   515→\tif deployment.Status.UpdatedReplicas != updatedReplicas {\n   516→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected .updatedReplicas: expect %d, got %d\", updatedReplicas, deployment.Status.UpdatedReplicas)\n   517→\t}\n   518→\tif deployment.Status.ReadyReplicas != readyReplicas {\n   519→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected .readyReplicas: expect %d, got %d\", readyReplicas, deployment.Status.ReadyReplicas)\n   520→\t}\n   521→\tif deployment.Status.AvailableReplicas != availableReplicas {\n   522→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected clientset.Interface, nodeName string, taints []v1.Taint) wait.ConditionWithContextFunc {\n\treturn func(context.Context) (bool, error) {\n\t\tnode, err := cs.CoreV1().Nodes().Get(ctx, nodeName, metav1.GetOptions{})\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn false, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// node.Spec.Taints may have more taints\n\t\tif len(taints) > len(node.Spec.Taints) {\n\t\t\treturn false, nil\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, taint := range taints {\n\t\t\tif !taintutils.TaintExists(node.Spec.Taints, &taint) {\n\t\t\t\treturn false, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn true, nil\n\t}\n}\n\n// NodeReadyStatus returns the status of first condition with type NodeReady.\n// If none of the condition is of type NodeReady, returns an error.\nfunc NodeReadyStatus(conditions []v1.NodeCondition) (v1.ConditionStatus, error) {\n\tfor _, c := range conditions {\n\t\tif c.Type != v1.NodeReady {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Just return the first condition with type NodeReady\n\t\treturn c.Status, nil\n\t}\n\treturn v1.ConditionFalse, errors.New(\"None of the conditions is of type NodeReady\")\n}\n\n// GetTolerationSeconds gets the period of time the toleration\nfunc WaitForReflection waits till the passFunc confirms that the object it expects\n// to see is in the store. Used to observe reflected events.\nfunc WaitForReflection(ctx context.Context, t *testing.T, nodeLister corelisters.NodeLister, key string,\n\tpassFunc func(n interface{}) bool) error {\n\tvar nodes []*v1.Node\n\terr := wait.PollUntilContextTimeout(ctx, time.Millisecond*100, wait.ForeverTestTimeout, false, func(context.Context) (bool, error) {\n\t\tn, err := nodeLister.Get(key)\n\n\t\tswitch {\n\t\tcase err == nil && passFunc(n):\n\t\t\treturn true, nil\n\t\tcase apierrors.IsNotFound(err):\n\t\t\tnodes = append(nodes, nil)\n\t\tcase err != nil:\n\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"Unexpected error: %v\", err)\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tnodes = append(nodes, n)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn false, nil\n\t})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Logf(\"Logging consecutive node versions received from store:\")\n\t\tfor i, n := range nodes {\n\t\t\tt.Logf(\"%d: %#v\", i, n)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn err\n}\n\nfunc UpdateNode(cs clientset.Interface, node *v1.Node) (*v1.Node, error) {\n\treturn error) {\n\t\tpod, err := c.CoreV1().Pods(podNamespace).Get(ctx, podName, metav1.GetOptions{})\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t// This could be a connection error so we want to retry.\n\t\t\treturn false, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tif pod.Spec.NodeName == \"\" {\n\t\t\treturn false, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor _, nodeName := range nodeNames {\n\t\t\tif pod.Spec.NodeName == nodeName {\n\t\t\t\treturn true, PodUnschedulable(c clientset.Interface, podNamespace, podName string) wait.ConditionWithContextFunc {\n\treturn func(ctx context.Context) (bool, error) {\n\t\tpod, err := c.CoreV1().Pods(podNamespace).Get(ctx, podName, metav1.GetOptions{})\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t// This could be a connection error so we want to retry.\n\t\t\treturn false, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\t_, cond nil\n\t}\n}\n\n// PodSchedulingError returns a condition function that returns true if the given pod\n// gets unschedulable status for reasons other than \"Unschedulable\". context.Context) (bool, error) {\n\t\tpod, err := c.CoreV1().Pods(podNamespace).Get(ctx, podName, metav1.GetOptions{})\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t// This could be a connection error so we want to v1.PodReasonUnschedulable, nil\n\t}\n}\n\n// PodSchedulingGated returns a condition function that returns true if the given pod\n// gets unschedulable status of reason 'SchedulingGated'.\nfunc
